endingPicker = (out, totv, aa, quickstats) => {

    function setImage(url) {
        if(url == '' || url == null) return;
        let interval = setInterval(function () {
            img = document.getElementsByClassName("person_image")[0];
            if (img != null) {
                img.src = url;
                clearInterval(interval);
            }
        }, 50);
    }

    if(quickstats[0] == 538) {
        setImage("https://i.imgur.com/SS3rpKB_d.webp?maxwidth=760&fidelity=grand");
        return `The Boykissing Act of 2030 enacted mandatory boykissing sessions in all 50 states and territories of the United States of America. The act was spearheaded by President Exeon as a part of their "Boy kissing" initiative that saw massive support from the populace in their 2028 Campaign. 

<p> The act requires that every first Monday of every month, all American citizens are required to go out and kiss at least 2 boys. While some scholars have argued that the act is unconstitutional, the Supreme Court has repeatedly struck down these arguments in cases such as <i> DeSantis v. Ethereal Shroom </i>. Governor Abbott pledged to repeal the law in his 2032 campaign, which played a large role in his landslide defeat.`;
    }
    if(quickstats[0] > 269) {
        setImage("");
        return `<h3>"We can now project that..." </h3><p> "Gunsmokexeon has been elected as the 48th President of the United States. This is a monumental occasion in American History, as Gunsmoke is the first ever LGBT+ person to ever be elected to the White House. In addition, it stands as a stunning rebuke of the Trump administration's policies over the last 4 years, primarily its conservative economic and social policies."`;
    }
    if(quickstats[0] < 270) {
        setImage("");
        return `<h3>"We can now project that..." </h3><p> "James David Vance has been elected as the 48th President of the United States. This is a historic moment in American History, as Vance will be the first ever Millennial President, potentially marking a shifting towards a younger generation in the American political system."`;
    }
}
